The given function is $c = -3n + 60$. To find the rate of change, we need to find the derivative of $c$ with respect to $n$.

The derivative of $c$ with respect to $n$ is given by:
$$\frac{dc}{dn} = \frac{d}{dn}(-3n + 60)$$

Using the power rule for differentiation, we get:
$$\frac{dc}{dn} = -3$$

Therefore, the rate of change described by this function is $\boxed{-3}$ people per tour. This corresponds to option $\boxed{\text{B)}}$.
